CREATE TABLE categories (category_id INT PRIMARY KEY, category_name STRING, parent_category_id INT REFERENCES categories(category_id))</t><s>UPSERT INTO users (id, name, email, date_of_birth) VALUES (1, 'John Doe', 'john.doe@example.com', '1990-01-01') ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET name = 'John Doe', email = 'john.doe@example.com', date_of_birth = '1990-01-01';</s>

CREATE TABLE accounts (account_id INT PRIMARY KEY, user_id INT REFERENCES users(id), account_type STRING, balance DECIMAL(10, 2))

CREATE TABLE categories (category_id INT PRIMARY KEY, category_name STRING, parent_category_id INT REFERENCES categories(category_id))</t><s>upsert into users (id, name, email, date_of_birth) values (1, 'john doe', 'john.doe@example.com', '1990-01-01') on conflict (id) do update set name = 'john doe', email = 'john.doe@example.com', date_of_birth = '1990-01-01';</s>

CREATE TABLE users (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name STRING, email STRING, date_of_birth DATE)</t><s>UPSERT INTO accounts (account_id, user_id, account_type, balance) VALUES (101, 1, 'Savings', 1000.00) ON CONFLICT (account_id) DO UPDATE SET user_id = 1, account_type = 'Savings', balance = 1000.00;</s>

CREATE TABLE budget (id INT PRIMARY KEY, user_id INT, category_id INT, amount DECIMAL(10, 2), month INT, year INT)

CREATE TABLE transactions (id INT PRIMARY KEY, account_id INT, transaction_type VARCHAR(10), amount DECIMAL(10, 2), date TIMESTAMP)

CREATE TABLE categories (id INT PRIMARY KEY, category_name VARCHAR(50))</t><s>upsert into users (id, name, email) values (1, 'john doe', 'john@example.com') on duplicate key update name='john doe', email='john@example.com';</s>

CREATE TABLE accounts (id INT PRIMARY KEY, user_id INT, account_name VARCHAR(50), balance DECIMAL(10, 2))

CREATE TABLE budget (id INT PRIMARY KEY, user_id INT, category_id INT, amount DECIMAL(10, 2), month INT, year INT)

CREATE TABLE users (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), email VARCHAR(50))</t><s>upsert into users (id, name, email) values (1, 'john doe', 'john@example.com') on duplicate key update name='john doe', email='john@example.com';</s>

CREATE TABLE transactions (id INT PRIMARY KEY, account_id INT, transaction_type VARCHAR(10), amount DECIMAL(10, 2), date TIMESTAMP)

CREATE TABLE budget (id INT PRIMARY KEY, user_id INT, category_id INT, amount DECIMAL(10, 2), month INT, year INT)

CREATE TABLE users (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), email VARCHAR(50))</t><s>UPSERT INTO accounts (id, user_id, account_name, balance) VALUES (1, 1, 'Savings Account', 1000.00) ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE user_id=1, account_name='Savings Account', balance=1000.00;</s>

CREATE TABLE transactions (id INT PRIMARY KEY, account_id INT, transaction_type VARCHAR(10), amount DECIMAL(10, 2), date TIMESTAMP)</t><s>UPSERT INTO transactions (id, account_id, transaction_type, amount, date) VALUES (1, 1, 'Deposit', 500.00, '2022-02-15 10:00:00') ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE account_id=1, transaction_type='Deposit', amount=500.00, date='2022-02-15 10:00:00';</s>
